</pre>
## Idea

A type is `π_n`-finite if it has finitely many connected components and all of its homotopy groups up to level `n` at all base points are finite.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="6689" class="Comment">-- Section 1. π-Finiteness</a>

<a id="6717" class="Comment">-- Definition 1.3</a>

<a id="6736" class="Comment">-- We introduce locally finite types</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-Prop"></a><a id="6774" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6774" class="Function">is-locally-finite-Prop</a> <a id="6797" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="6801" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6802" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6802" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6804" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6806" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6811" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6813" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6815" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6818" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6802" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6820" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6822" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1393" class="Function">UU-Prop</a> <a id="6830" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6802" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="6832" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6774" class="Function">is-locally-finite-Prop</a> <a id="6855" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6855" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6857" class="Symbol">=</a>

  <a id="8586" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#5874" class="Function">prod-Prop</a> <a id="8596" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8598" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8427" class="Function">is-π-finite-Prop</a> <a id="8615" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1569" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="8622" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8580" class="Bound">X</a><a id="8623" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="8637" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8639" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#6694" class="Function">Π-Prop</a> <a id="8646" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8580" class="Bound">X</a>
              <a id="8662" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8664" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="8666" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8666" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8668" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8670" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#6694" class="Function">Π-Prop</a> <a id="8677" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8580" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="8679" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8682" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8682" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8684" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8686" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8427" class="Function">is-π-finite-Prop</a> <a id="8703" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8577" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8705" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8706" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1767" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="8709" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8666" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8711" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8682" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8712" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="9286" class="Comment">-- Basic properties of locally finite types</a>

<a id="9331" class="Comment">-- locally finite types are closed under equivalences</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-equiv"></a><a id="9386" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9386" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9410" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9414" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9415" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9415" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="9418" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9418" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="9421" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9423" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9428" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9430" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9431" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9431" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9433" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9435" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9438" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9415" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="9440" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9442" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9443" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9443" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9445" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9447" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9450" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9418" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="9452" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9454" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9455" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9455" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9459" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9431" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9461" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="9463" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9443" class="Bound">B</a><a id="9464" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9466" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="9470" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6920" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9488" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9443" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9490" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9492" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6920" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9510" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9431" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="9512" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9386" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9536" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9536" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9538" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9538" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9540" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9540" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9542" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9542" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9544" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="9548" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#6576" class="Function">is-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9565" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9566" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#16746" class="Function">equiv-ap</a> <a id="9575" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9536" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9577" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9540" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9579" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9542" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9580" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9582" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9583" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9538" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9585" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9586" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="9596" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9536" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9598" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9540" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9599" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9601" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9602" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="9612" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9536" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9614" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9542" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9615" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;"></a><a id="9619" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9619" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9644" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9648" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9649" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9649" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="9652" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9652" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="9655" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9657" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9662" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9664" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9665" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9665" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9667" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9669" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9672" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9649" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="9674" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9676" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9677" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9677" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9679" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9681" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9684" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9652" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="9686" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9688" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9689" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9689" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9691" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9693" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9665" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9695" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="9697" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9677" class="Bound">B</a><a id="9698" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9700" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="9704" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6920" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9722" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9665" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9724" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9726" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6920" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9744" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9677" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="9746" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9619" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9771" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9771" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9773" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9775" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9386" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9799" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9800" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5721" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="9810" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9771" class="Bound">e</a><a id="9811" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="9814" class="Comment">-- types with decidable equality are locally finite</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-has-decidable-equality"></a><a id="9867" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9867" class="Function">is-locally-finite-has-decidable-equality</a> <a id="9908" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="19834" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4139" class="Function">is-finite</a> <a id="19844" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#19803" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19846" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19848" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="19850" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#19850" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="19852" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19854" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#19803" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19855" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19857" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19859" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8718" class="Function">is-π-finite</a> <a id="19871" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#19795" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="19873" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19874" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#19815" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="19876" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#19850" class="Bound">a</a><a id="19877" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19880" class="Symbol">→</a>
